# Operation Log

Chronological record of significant operations. Each entry is its own file under `log/`; this page is the reverse-chronological index. See [concepts/parallel-session-coordination.md](concepts/parallel-session-coordination.md) for why.

- [2026-05-25 — Observe need card: whole-tile Open button + top-right "x" dismiss confirm](log/2026-05-25-observe-need-card-as-button-x-dismiss.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture` (`bf65f407`, 2 files +136/−60). Interaction polish on the "Open Observation Needs" carousel (`OpenObservationNeedsPanel`, route `observe/command-centre`). **(1) Card-as-button:** dropped the standalone "Open" button — the whole tile is the launch trigger (`role="button"`+`tabIndex=0`+`aria-label`, `onClick→onLaunch`, Enter/Space `onKeyDown`); a `<div>` not `<button>` so inner controls stay valid nested interactives. **(2) X-dismiss confirm:** auto needs' one-click Dismiss → a top-right **×** (`.cardDismiss`) that opens a two-step inline **"Dismiss?" · Dismiss · Cancel** (reuses the manual-need "Remove?" confirm classes); Dismiss = `setStatus … 'resolved'`. Every inner control (`×`/Edit/Remove/confirm buttons) `stopPropagation` so it never fires the card's launch; the `.objCardActions` footer renders only when editable **or** an auto card is mid-confirm (seed cards = no footer). New `confirmDismissId` state + `dismissNeed` handler; **model/store/schema unchanged** — only the surface moved. **Verified live** (:5200, DOM/eval): 15 cards all `role="button"`, 0 Open buttons, × on the 7 auto cards only; body-click + Enter both launch the capture workspace; × doesn't navigate + shows "Dismiss?"; Cancel restores (15), Dismiss resolves (15→14). `typecheck` clean for both files (5 errors are the known foreign-WIP baseline; `preview_screenshot` times out on MapLibre WebGL — stated not claimed). No new ADR (interaction polish). Foreign WIP untouched per [[feedback-no-deletion]]; explicit-path commit per [[feedback-commit-immediately-on-rebased-branches]]. Follows [[log/2026-05-25-observe-command-centre-polish-edit-delete-clamp-contrast]].
- [2026-05-25 — Blob-sync ramp Stage 2: operator A–E matrix, best-effort auto-drive](log/2026-05-25-blobsync-stage2-operator-matrix-autodrive.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Stage 2 of the `FLAGS.SYNC_STATE_BLOBS` ramp, **best-effort auto-drive** on an `e6b48857`-inclusive build: migrated throwaway Postgres (`postgis:16-3.4`, 5433) + API (3001) + a genuinely flag-on web preview (5205), driving the Phase 5 ADR **§5.7** matrix through the live browser. **Central blocker fixed:** the build came up **flag-off** because the `.claude/launch.json` `web-sync` entry used `set "VAR=true" && …` — the **inner double-quotes break under the preview launcher's `cmd /c` spawn**, silently dropping the env var (the `process.env` access + vite `define` were already correct; purely env delivery). Fixed to quote-free `set FEATURE_SYNC_STATE_BLOBS=true&& …` → runtime `FLAGS.SYNC_STATE_BLOBS: true` (the prior session's pre-fix A-shadow was on a flag-off build, redone here). **Results:** **A — shadow PASS** (3 stores spanning `byProject`+`projectId-tagged` scopes; store edit → 800ms-debounced subscribe → PUT 200 → physical `jsonb_typeof=object` rows under the right `(project_id,store_key)`; final site-profiles rev2/swot rev4/vision rev2). **B — restore PASS** (clean local + reload → hydrate applies all slices + seeds `blobBaseRev`; cross-project read isolation rests on Stage-1 case B, only one live project in-browser). **C — conflict PASS** (genuine cross-device 409 via out-of-band `curl` PUT → stale browser edit → 409 `{serverRev,serverPayload}`; Connectivity-panel chip + `toast.warning`; local **not** clobbered, server unchanged; recovery edit bumps rev — surface is the chip+toast = `OfflineBanner` `conflictedStores>0` branch, not a standalone red bar). **D — skew NOT RUN** (operator-only; needs a higher-schema second build). **E — bundle relabel PASS** ("syncs to your account" present; Export/Import enabled; `buildBundle`+`serializeBundle` → valid ~332KB bundle; `parseBundle` present). `preview_screenshot` not used (MapLibre WebGL times out — stated not claimed); evidence is browser-eval/console/network + direct DB `SELECT`s. **Ramp impact:** A/B/C/E green; flip still gated on the genuine two-physical-device sign-off + D-skew; **Stages 3 (soak) + 4 (flip) remain gated/unexecuted** (`flags.ts`/`vite.config.ts` untouched). launch.json edit touched only the `web-sync` entry, foreign WIP intact per [[feedback-no-deletion]]; DB torn down. ADR [[decisions/2026-05-17-atlas-syncservice-coverage-phase5]] §5.7 Stage-2 addendum. Follows [[log/2026-05-25-blobsync-stage1-validation-two-latent-bugs]].

- [2026-05-25 — Blob-sync ramp Stage 1: real-Postgres validation surfaces two flip-blocking bugs](log/2026-05-25-blobsync-stage1-validation-two-latent-bugs.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`, commit `e6b48857` (2 files, +20/−4). First run of `blobSync.integration` (cases A/B/C) against a **live Postgres** for Stage 1 of the `FLAGS.SYNC_STATE_BLOBS` ramp — caught two latent `/project-state` route bugs the FIFO-mock suites cannot see. **(1)** `rev` (`BIGINT`) comes back from postgres.js as a **string**, failing `ProjectStateBlob.parse` (`z.number`) → **422 on every successful PUT**; coerced in `parseRow`. **(2)** the PUT pre-stringified then cast `::jsonb`, **double-encoding** the payload into a jsonb string scalar (`jsonb_typeof = string`); the client does no `JSON.parse` so hydration would load stores with a string — fixed with `${db.json(...)}::jsonb` (serialize once). Also fixed the spec's project INSERTs to supply `org_id` (NOT NULL since migration 036) by resolving the register-time personal org. Infra: the compose container on 5432 was shadowed by a host-native PG17 on IPv4 5432, sidestepped via a throwaway `postgis:16-3.4` on **5433** (fresh volume → auto-migrate), torn down after. Verified: integration **A/B/C 3/3** real Postgres; mock `projectState` 6/6 + `vegetationSuccession` 8/8 (no regression); `@ogden/api` `tsc` exit 0. **Ramp impact:** the flag was **not flip-ready** before `e6b48857`; Stage 1 gate now green, Stages 2 (operator matrix), 3 (soak), 4 (flip) remain gated. Explicit-path commit, foreign WIP untouched per [[feedback-no-deletion]]. Follows [[log/2026-05-25-versioned-blob-skip-dev-observability]].
- [2026-05-25 — Two Observe bug fixes: waterRouter type baseline + Command Centre hidden tray](log/2026-05-25-command-centre-tray-and-waterrouter-fixes.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Two small plan-mode fixes. **(1) `fabf3e38`** — `ObserveAnnotationLayers.tsx` TS7053 baseline: the `LayerSpec.toggleKey` `Exclude` union had drifted out of sync with the `subToggles` `Record` after the store added `waterRouter` (a Plan-stage overlay, `matrixTogglesStore` v14); `subToggles[spec.toggleKey]` widened to `any`. Added `'waterRouter'` to the union so both resolve to the same key set (`topography, sectors, zones, water, builtEnvironment, scheduledMoves`) — **type-only, zero runtime**; baseline dropped 6→4. **(2) `f2a88288`** — the "Open Observation Needs" carousel was pushed below the viewport fold; root cause was a **grid track/child mismatch** from parallel-session `996d2948` (dropped `.topbar` → 3 children, but `grid-template-rows` still had **4** tracks), so `.body` landed in an `auto` track and content-sized to map height (mapRegion 420px) instead of flex-filling, shoving the tray off-screen. **CSS-only** fix: `grid-template-rows: auto minmax(0,1fr) auto` (tabs/body/tray) — no JSX/store/behaviour change; responsive block unaffected. Verified by DOM bounding-box reads (tray bottom 463 ≤ winH 475; `preview_screenshot` times out on MapLibre WebGL — **stated, not claimed**). Both explicit-path commits, foreign WIP untouched per [[feedback-no-deletion]], divergence-checked before push per [[feedback-commit-immediately-on-rebased-branches]]. No new ADR (bug fixes; the grid fix is a regression repair to `996d2948`). Continues [[entities/web-app]] Observe Command Centre thread.
- [2026-05-25 — Versioned-blob push: make the serverId-less skip observable in dev](log/2026-05-25-versioned-blob-skip-dev-observability.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture` (`05096b06`, 1 file +17/−1). Follow-up to the syncManifest backfill: registration alone didn't prove the 7 new stores *round-trip*, and the prior "known issue" line (`initialSync` 401s for non-UUID demo projects like `mtc`) was **inaccurate**. Plan-mode investigation: the client never sends a non-UUID id — `enqueueVersionedBlob` (`syncService.ts:1216`) **silently returns** when the active project has no `serverId`, so `mtc` is skipped *before* any request (no 401); `mtc` is also a **builtin** → RBAC viewer-only → blob PUT rejected even with a UUID, so minting one wouldn't help; and the whole loop is **default-off** behind `FLAGS.SYNC_STATE_BLOBS` (`flags.ts:19`). So **no server/DB/RBAC/validation change** — the gap is observability + test method. **Change:** the no-`serverId` skip now emits a **dev-only, de-duped** `console.info` (`import.meta.env.DEV` + module-level `warnedNoServerId` Set → once per project) explaining builtin/demo projects are viewer-only and to use a created/owned project; prod byte-identical. Dev enables the loop with `$env:FEATURE_SYNC_STATE_BLOBS='true'; npm run dev` (env var already wired by `vite.config.ts:170`; `flags.ts` default + `define` block untouched so `syncFlagWiring.test.ts` stays green). **Verified:** `syncManifestRoundTrip.test.ts` 76/76 (table-driven, auto-covers the 7 stores' select↔apply + isolation) + `syncManifest.test.ts` 10/10 = **86 passed**; `tsc --noEmit` **exit 0** (8GB heap). Not browser-observable (queue console log); manual two-browser round-trip left to steward. Plan-approved before edit; explicit-path commit, foreign WIP untouched per [[feedback-no-deletion]], divergence-checked (0 behind/1 ahead) per [[feedback-commit-immediately-on-rebased-branches]] (first push blocked by auto-mode classifier, sent on explicit "push"). Plan: `~/.claude/plans/resolve-the-non-uuid-demo-project-tidy-leaf.md`. Continues [[entities/web-app]] syncManifest thread.

- [2026-05-25 — Compass toast reads real How-checks, not seed evidence](log/2026-05-25-compass-toast-reads-real-checks.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture` (`73ff75a0`, 3 files). See ADR [[2026-05-25-atlas-compass-toast-reads-real-checks]]. Steward screenshot bug: the Observe **HUMAN CONTEXT** panel read **"33% · 1/3 steps"** (only the last How checkbox ticked) yet the in-map **"Objective complete"** toast fired — "Just because the last task on the list is marked complete it renders the whole objective as complete." Chose to fix **all three stages** (AskUserQuestion). **Root cause:** two parallel progress systems read different sources — the visible panel (`GuidanceCard` via `*ChecklistAside`) uses `progressFromChecks(checked, how.length)` over the **real** per-stage How-checks store (→1/3 ✓), but the toast (`*ObjectiveCompletePrompt` via the single-objective hooks `use*ObjectiveProgress`) used `objectiveProgress` over the **seed-backed compass** store, where `isVerified = raw[i]==='verified' || checked.includes(i)`; the Observe `human-context` SEED `{0:'verified',1:'verified',2:'evidence-in'}` + the one real tick on node 2 = 3/3 = 100% → false toast. Purely SEED-as-completion, not a count mismatch (`nodes.length === how.length` since compass nodes are `how.map(...)`). **Fix (3 files, −12 net):** repoint each single-objective hook (`useCompassData.ts`/`usePlanCompassData.ts`/`useActCompassData.ts`) to `progressFromChecks(checks ?? EMPTY_CHECKS, obj.nodes.length)`, dropping the `seedFor` evidence read + `evidence` dep; compass-store imports stay (the plural `use*CompassData` **wheel** hook still uses SEED for its prototype). Toast components unchanged (their `pct===100` gate is correct once fed real numbers). **Verified in-browser** (:5200): Observe 1/3→no toast (screenshot), 3/3→toast (screenshot), untick→toast gone; Plan `livestock` 2/4→no toast, 4/4→toast; Act `tracker` seed-gap analog (SEED verifies 0+1) driven via localStorage — node-2-only→no toast, 3/3→toast (screenshot), test state cleaned up. `objectiveStatus.test.ts` 10/10; `tsc` clean for the 3 files (only the **known 3-error foreign-WIP baseline** remains — `StepBoundary.tsx`, two `HostUnion*` tests; `tsc` OOMs at default heap, re-ran with `--max-old-space-size=8192`). Staged by **explicit path** per [[feedback-commit-immediately-on-rebased-branches]], foreign WIP untouched per [[feedback-no-deletion]], divergence-checked (1 ahead/0 behind) before push.
- [2026-05-25 — Plan rail: hide the project-level readiness cue when an objective is focused](log/2026-05-25-plan-ready-cue-hide-when-focused.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture` (`862fdf08`, 1 file). Steward flagged the **"Plan essentials · 17%"** card (`PlanReadyCue`) as "goes against focus of chosen objective in this view" — it stayed pinned atop the Plan right rail even after an objective was focused, competing with that objective's own workspace. **Root cause:** the rail (`PlanLayout.tsx:~471`) stacked **two** components unconditionally — the *project-level* `PlanReadyCue` (reads `usePlanProgress(projectId)`, not the focused objective) above the *objective-aware* `PlanChecklistAside` (which shows "No objective selected" when `activeModule === null`, else the objective workspace). **Fix:** gate the cue on `validModule === null` (the same "objective focused" signal the aside uses) so it renders **only** in the no-objective state; once an objective is focused the rail belongs entirely to its workspace. **Verified** (DOM probe; `preview_screenshot` times out on WebGL, stated not claimed): `/plan` → cue present ("Plan essentials · 17%") + "No objective selected"; `/plan/water-management` → cue absent, workspace fills the rail. **Ownership caveat:** `PlanReadyCue`/`PlanLayout.tsx` are the **parallel session's** WIP (commit `047c06f9`) on the foreign-WIP exclusion list — changed at the steward's explicit direction, committed immediately by explicit path per [[feedback-commit-immediately-on-rebased-branches]], divergence-checked (0 behind/1 ahead) before push (`291a6ff2..862fdf08`); possible conflict flagged.
- [2026-05-25 — Compass progress fill: outside-in (rim → centre)](log/2026-05-25-compass-progress-fill-outside-in.md) — **Branch.** atlas `feat/atlas-permaculture` (`d181f223`, 2 files) + `ogden-ui-components` `release/v0.1.1`/tag `v0.1.1` (`e71fcc3`). Steward, looking at the **True North** compass, asked each progress wedge to **fill from the outer rim inward toward the hub** as completion rises (full wedge at 100%, sliver at the rim near 0%), reversing the prior centre→rim fill. **The non-obvious part: the wheel isn't in atlas.** It's the shared `MaqasidComparisonWheel` in the separate repo `@ogden/ui-components`, consumed as a **pinned GitHub tarball** whose `dist/` is **committed** — so the fix is a cross-repo release: edit source + rebuild/commit `dist/` in the component repo, then bump atlas's pin. **Steward decisions (AskUserQuestion):** (a) **surgical patch v0.1.1** off the `v0.1.0` tag (avoids pulling intervening additive BBOS/educational components into atlas); (b) **all wheels** — flip once in the shared component, no opt-in prop. **The change = 3 lines, one file:** the existing `annularSector(rInner, rOuter,…)` helper already takes both radii, so progress flips from a *moving outer* radius (`currentR = HUB_R + (PROGRESS_MAX_R-HUB_R)·pct`) to a *moving inner* radius (`fillInnerR = PROGRESS_MAX_R - (PROGRESS_MAX_R-HUB_R)·pct`; `HUB_R=56`, `PROGRESS_MAX_R=142`), with the `mcw-seg-current` fill + `mcw-seg-pattern` overlay drawn as `annularSector(fillInnerR, PROGRESS_MAX_R,…)`. Dim track / 0%-empty ring / complete-arc / gradient / entrance animation untouched — **no CSS change**. **Blast radius = 5 atlas surfaces** (True North, Observe, Plan, Act, OPA dashboard wheel); the separate `CycleWheel` is out of scope. **Release+pin:** branched from `v0.1.0`, `npm run build` regenerated dist, committed source+dist (`e71fcc3`), tagged+pushed; atlas pin `#v0.1.0`→`#v0.1.1` (root `package.json` only; `apps/web` doesn't pin), `corepack pnpm install` → lockfile resolves `e71fcc3`. **Verification:** `preview_screenshot` times out (MapLibre/WebGL, **stated not claimed**); verified by a deterministic geometry probe of the **installed** minified bundle — fill resolves to `a = H - (H - B)·(i/100)` with `H=142`/`B=56` and the path call `annularSector(a, H,…)`, i.e. outer pinned at 142, inner tracks pct (142 at 0% → 56 at 100%); conclusive since geometry is a pure fn of pct. Atlas staged by **explicit path** (`package.json`+`pnpm-lock.yaml`), foreign WIP untouched per [[feedback-no-deletion]], divergence-checked before push per [[feedback-commit-immediately-on-rebased-branches]]. **Addendum — "wheel looks unchanged" root cause + forward-port:** the steward then reported the wheel looked the same; investigation found the code was correct but the app **served stale pixels** — (1) the **v0.1.1 release never bumped `package.json` `version`** (stuck at `0.1.0`), so caches had no invalidation signal *(the real defect)*, and (2) atlas's `optimizeDeps.exclude` serves the dep raw and vite **doesn't watch `node_modules`**, so the dev server running since before the install kept its old transform. **Fix:** restart the dev server + clear `apps/web/node_modules/.vite`; DOM-probe then confirmed outer arc fixed at 142 / inner tracks pct = rim→centre (`preview_screenshot` times out on WebGL, stated not claimed). **Lesson:** *a release must bump `package.json` `version`, not just move a tag.* **Forward-port done:** same 3-line flip applied to `ogden-ui-components` `main`, `version` bumped 0.3.0→**0.3.1** (defect not repeated), dist rebuilt (diff limited to the `index` bundles + maps), committed by explicit path, **tagged `v0.3.1`**, pushed (`46a1815..90aa7c6`). v0.1.1 left intact; atlas pin-to-v0.3.1 noted as non-blocking follow-up. **Addendum — atlas pin bumped v0.1.1 → v0.3.1 (`77fe24af`):** closed that follow-up — pin `#v0.1.1`→`#v0.3.1` so atlas now carries the **correct `version` field** (0.3.1), closing the cache-busting defect; same wheel geometry, plus additive BBOS/educational (zero bundle impact — atlas imports only the wheel/hover-store/LevelNavigator, BBOS is a separate dist entry). **The gotcha:** v0.3.x changed the dist from single-file (`dist/ogden-ui-components.es.js`) to **multi-entry** (`dist/index.es.js` + `dist/bbos.es.js`), and atlas resolves via a hardcoded **vite alias** (not the `exports` map), so the alias was repointed `dist/ogden-ui-components.es.js`→`dist/index.es.js` (CSS alias unchanged — same filename). **Verified:** installed `version` = 0.3.1; `dist/index.es.js` carries `a = H - (H - V)·(i/100)` drawn `ue(a,H,…)`; live wheel DOM-probe outer-fixed-142/inner-tracks-pct (rim→centre); `vite build` resolves the repointed alias in 39.5s (the `tsc && vite build` script's `tsc` step fails on the known 3-error foreign-WIP baseline — ran `vite build` directly). Explicit-path commit (`package.json`+`apps/web/vite.config.ts`+`pnpm-lock.yaml`), foreign WIP untouched, divergence-checked. Plan: `~/.claude/plans/light-mode-of-the-splendid-crayon.md` (Parts 4–6).
- [2026-05-24 — Header spine shows real Plan/Act % (drop the em dash)](log/2026-05-24-header-stage-spine-plan-act-pct.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Follow-up to [[log/2026-05-24-header-stage-spine]] taking its deferred item: the header `StageSpine`'s **Plan/Act** segments showed an em dash (`—`) while **Observe** showed its real verified %; the dash was retained only because Plan/Act were believed to lack a header progress source. They don't — the post-refactor compass gives each stage its own data hook (`usePlanCompassData` / `useActCompassData`), each returning the same `.stage` aggregate the Observe hook already feeds. Steward directed the dash be replaced. **All three segments now show a live `%` from their own compass data;** routing behaviour unchanged. **Supersedes locked decision #1** of the header-spine ADR (recorded as an Addendum there). **How:** `StageSpine`'s `observeProgress: ObjectiveProgress` prop → `progressByStage: Record<Stage, ObjectiveProgress>`, per-segment readout now the uniform `` `${progressByStage[stage.id].pct}%` `` (Observe-only special-case + em-dash branch removed); still purely presentational + consumed only by `HeaderStageSpine`, so the prop-shape change is fully contained. `HeaderStageSpine` calls all three hooks **unconditionally** before the off-route early return (each calls its Zustand selectors + a single `useMemo` → rules-of-hooks safe), builds `progressByStage = { observe: observeData.stage, plan: planData.stage, act: actData.stage }`; the Observe-by-progress routing branch unchanged (`observeData.stage.pct >= 100`). **Covenant clean** — pure presentation, no schema/store/model/`MODULE_CARDS`/migration. **Verification:** `StageSpine.test.tsx` (6) + `HeaderStageSpine.test.tsx` (9 — one added asserting each segment renders its own mocked %) green (15/15), em-dash assertions removed; `tsc --noEmit` at the 3-error pre-existing baseline (`StepBoundary.tsx` `ReactNode`; two `HostUnion*` test types). - [2026-05-24 — MapLibre marker hover fix + temporary Command Centre unlock](log/2026-05-24-marker-hover-fix-and-command-centre-unlock.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Two small compass/map touch-ups. **(1) Bug fix `80f2b9d3`:** hovering a Command Centre objective marker made it jump to the map's top-left corner. Root cause — MapLibre writes the *entire* positioning `transform` (`translate(-50%,-50%) translate(x,y)…`) onto a DOM marker's own element each frame; the `mouseenter` handler set `el.style.transform = 'scale(...)'` on that **same** element, erasing the translate → marker snapped to the container origin until the next position write. Fix: move the hover scale to an inner `pin` child (`line-height:0` outer shrink-wraps it; geometry unchanged, clicks bubble); fixed in both `ObjectiveMapMarkers.tsx` (reported) and `FieldFlagOverlay.tsx` (identical pattern). Other DOM-marker overlays don't hover-transform (grep-verified). **Reusable lesson: never write `transform` on a MapLibre marker element — scale an inner child.** **(2) Temp unlock `e615c6da`:** steward asked to enter the Observe Command Centre without all objectives verified; the center-unlock gate ([[decisions/2026-05-24-atlas-observe-command-centre]]) is one `ready` flag in `StageCompassPage.tsx` driving the wheel hotspot's clickability + `forceConverged` glow + `onEnter()`. Forced `ready = data.views.length > 0`, marked **TEMP** with the exact one-line revert in a comment. Both pure presentation/behaviour — covenant clean, no schema/store/model/migration. `tsc` at the 3-error pre-existing baseline; committed by name per [[feedback-commit-immediately-on-rebased-branches]]; live preview not run (MapLibre canvas hangs screenshots — documented standard).
- [2026-05-24 — Scope Act map overlays to the active objective](log/2026-05-24-act-map-overlay-scoping.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`, commit `49c22d27` (2 files). Closes the **deferred-Act** gap from [[decisions/2026-05-24-atlas-single-objective-map-overlay-focus]] (its decision 4: "Plan only, defer Act"). - [2026-05-22 — Plan/Observe follow-ups: maplibre line-width fix + URL-persist picked section](log/2026-05-22-plan-observe-followups-linewidth-url-persist.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closed the two deferred follow-ups from [[log/2026-05-22-cross-rail-single-section-highlight]] (`fc0938b8`). **Part 1 — `design-el-line` line-width** (`apps/web/src/v3/plan/canvas/layers/DesignElementLayers.tsx`): the layer threw `paint.line-width: Only one zoom-based "step" or "interpolate" subexpression may be used` **every frame**, because a zoom-based `lineWidthExpr` was nested inside a `case` **and** referenced twice (`['case', selFlag, ['+', lineWidthExpr, 2], lineWidthExpr]`) — two nested zoom curves. MapLibre requires the zoom curve to be the **outermost** expression of a paint property (only the *input* must be `['zoom']`; feature-state is allowed in stop *outputs*). Fix: collapsed to a **single top-level** zoom `interpolate` with the `selFlag` `+2px` selection delta folded into each stop output; dropped the `case` wrap. Console buffer now clean of the error. **Part 2 — URL-persist `?section=`** (`PlanLayout.tsx` + `ObserveLayout.tsx`): moved `activeSectionId` from per-Layout `useState` to a URL **search param** (`useSearch({ strict:false }) as { section?: string }`), so the single-section cross-rail highlight survives reloads/back-forward/shared links. **No `validateSearch`** added — matches the `ObserveDeepLinkFocus` convention and avoids stripping the existing `focus*` deep-link params. Navigation collapsed into one `navigateModuleSection(mod, sectionId)` primitive writing the `$module` path + `?section` atomically (`navigate`'s `search` *replaces*, so passed explicitly every time); `handleSelectModule`→`(mod,null)` (whole family), `handleSelectSection` toggles on strict identity; PlanLayout's silvopasture-drilldown effect navigate also got `search:{}`. The four rail components are unchanged (already consume `effectiveSectionId`+`onSelectSection`). **Verification:** `cd apps/web && npm run typecheck` at the **3-error pre-existing baseline** (`StepBoundary.tsx`, two `HostUnion*` tests); live DOM/URL evals (:5200) — Plan cold-load `?section=be-agricultural`→2 active (survives reload), click narrows+writes `?section`, click active deselects+drops module&section (0), no-section→family (10); Observe `?section=be-building`→2, `be-from-map`→1 (main rail only, documented), no-section→family (13), live click writes `?section`. **Screenshot blocker root-cause corrected:** the prior session blamed the line-width error for the `preview_screenshot` 30 s timeout — **wrong.** With the error gone the screenshot still times out because the preview tab is **backgrounded** (`document.visibilityState==='hidden'`, `hasFocus()===false`), which throttles `requestAnimationFrame` so any frame-dependent op hangs while synchronous evals return instantly; `preview_resize` didn't foreground it. So the blocker is an **environment** condition (preview pane not focused), not renderer saturation and not the line-width bug — stated not assumed per the preview-verification rule; synchronous DOM/URL evals are authoritative here. Staged only the 3 files by explicit path; foreign WIP (EconomicsPanel, capitalPartner, SectorCompassOverlay, ZoneSomSidebar) untouched per `feedback_no_deletion`. Plan: `~/.claude/plans/the-sector-compass-in-memoized-sphinx.md`.

Generalizes the committed Plan-main-rail fix (`97182e38`, the "Plan rail single-section highlight" entry below) to **full cross-rail parity** with the steward-chosen **shared cross-rail state**: a section pick in the main rail propagates into the mini rail and vice-versa, so a stage shows exactly **one** active section everywhere (no "family-lit on arrival"). Before this, three rails still multi-lit — the **Observe main rail** (`ObserveTools`, three section families all routing to `built-environment`, lighting up to 7), and **both mini rails** (`PlanChecklistAside` / `ObserveChecklistAside`, `GuidanceCard`s keyed on `activeModule === routed`, so every BE card sharing a module lit together; Plan also has the machinery 2-way + structures-subsystems 5-way fan-out). **Approach: lift the section discriminator into each Layout** (mirroring the existing `slideUpOpen` lift), not a new store and no route-schema change. Each `*Layout` owns `activeSectionId: useState<string|null>` reconciled **lazily at render** into `effectiveSectionId = activeSectionId && sectionIdModule(activeSectionId) === validModule ? activeSectionId : null` (a stale id from reload / bottom-bar nav / deselect / the pre-navigate transient routes to a different module → ignored, so no race-prone `useEffect`). Three handlers split the former one: `navigateModule` (pure nav), `handleSelectModule` (`setActiveSectionId(null)` + nav — bottom bar / programmatic, clears narrow → whole family), `handleSelectSection` (toggle on strict identity — narrow/switch/deselect). Both `effectiveSectionId` + `onSelectSection` thread to **both** rails. **Uniform `isActive` in all four rails:** `effectiveSectionId !== null ? effectiveSectionId === sectionId : activeModule === routed` (`=== mod` for module sections); section ids reuse each section's React `key` (`mod`, `be-${category}`, `be-from-map`). **8 files:** 2 **new** centralized section maps (`plan/planSectionMap.ts`, `observe/observeSectionMap.ts` — each moves the formerly-duplicated `BE_CATEGORY_TO_*_MODULE` out of two rail files + adds a `*SectionIdModule(id)` helper; Observe's special-cases `be-from-map` **before** the be-slice) + 6 edited rail/Layout files (`PlanLayout`, `ObserveLayout`, `PlanTools`, `ObserveTools`, `PlanChecklistAside`, `ObserveChecklistAside`). **`GuidanceCard.tsx` unchanged** — its `onSelect` already fires only on inactive cards, exactly right under shared state. **Documented accepted behavior:** Observe "From map" sets `effectiveSectionId='be-from-map'` which matches no mini-rail card → mini rail shows **no** active card for that pick (it's a generic adopt meta-tool, not a BE category); a **cold URL load** with no prior click → family fallback (URL-persist is out of scope). **Verification:** `cd apps/web && npm run typecheck` at the **3-error pre-existing baseline** (`StepBoundary.tsx`, two `HostUnion*` tests), none in the 8 files; live DOM (Claude Preview :5200) `.groupActive` counts — Plan Agricultural→2, Buildings→2 (switch), active again→0 (deselect), Water Management (non-shared)→2, bottom-bar Structures→family 10; machinery module-level vs `be-machinery` each light alone; Observe Buildings→2, From map→1 (main only, documented), human-context→2. **Screenshot blocked by a pre-existing unrelated maplibre bug** (`DesignElementLayers.tsx` emits `paint.line-width: Only one zoom-based "step" or "interpolate" subexpression may be used` every frame, saturating the renderer → `preview_screenshot` 30 s timeout) — **not introduced here**; stated not assumed per the preview-verification rule, DOM counts authoritative. Staged only the 8 files by explicit path; concurrent-session foreign WIP untouched per `feedback_no_deletion`. Plan: `~/.claude/plans/the-sector-compass-in-memoized-sphinx.md`.

- [2026-05-22 — Client-error telemetry: `api_client` source wired (sink complete)](log/2026-05-22-client-error-telemetry-api-client-source.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Commit `004e4ad7`. Closes the last gap from [the sources-wired session](log/2026-05-21-client-error-telemetry-sources-wired.md): the `client_error_events` sink has **four** `source` values and the fourth, **`api_client`**, was still dark — API failures surfaced only as thrown `ApiError`s + uncaught network rejections, invisible server-side. **Scope (operator-confirmed):** report **all** failures (every `ApiError` incl. 401, **and** network/offline `fetch` rejections as `status:0`/`code:'NETWORK_ERROR'`, re-thrown unchanged); always-on **loop guard** excludes `/api/v1/telemetry/*` so a failed client-errors POST can't report itself; deliberate `AbortError`s skipped. **`apiClient.ts`** gains reporter-injection plumbing mirroring `setSessionExpiredHandler` (`ApiClientErrorReport` + `setApiClientErrorReporter` + private `reportApiFailure`); `request()` now wraps `fetch` in try/catch (reports non-abort rejections, re-throws original) and reports at the `ApiError` throw site before throwing. **Bundle-split preserved** — apiClient does **not** import `clientErrorLog` (would cycle, since clientErrorLog imports `api`, and drag the buffer into always-mounted code per [[decisions/2026-05-21-atlas-showcase-bundle-split]]); instead **`bootAuthed.ts`** (authed-only) registers the bridge `setApiClientErrorReporter((r) => recordClientError({ source:'api_client', ... }))`, `projectId` omitted so the active-project resolver stamps it. `stack`/`details` deliberately omitted (uninformative / payload-lean / no body leak). **Tests:** new `apiClient.clientError.test.ts` (happy-dom, stubbed `fetch`, spy reporter) — 6/6 green (5xx reported, 401 reported, network reported+rethrown, AbortError not reported, loop guard, no-reporter safe); web tsc shows only the 3 pre-existing unrelated baseline errors. **Follow-up (same day, commits `82d2bb19` code + `0f86be26` wiki):** the two upload throw sites are now wired too — `files.upload` (XHR) gains a `fail()` helper reporting each `ApiError` reject site (non-2xx `onload`, parse `catch`, `onerror`), and `regenerationEvents.uploadMedia` (fetch) became `async` with the same try/catch-around-fetch + report-before-throw pattern as `request()`; 4 new test cases (XHR stub + fetch mock) → 10/10 green, tsc baseline unchanged. **Every API failure path now emits `api_client` telemetry — no dark paths remain.** ADR back-links: [[decisions/2026-05-21-atlas-showcase-bundle-split]], [[log/2026-05-21-client-error-telemetry-sources-wired]].

- [2026-05-21 — Client-error telemetry: react_error_boundary + unhandled_rejection wired, migration 039 applied](log/2026-05-21-client-error-telemetry-sources-wired.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Direct follow-up to [the client-error telemetry sink](log/2026-05-21-client-error-telemetry-sink.md), which shipped `recordClientError` + the buffered POST pipeline + the `client_error_events` table but left three of its four `source` enum values unused. This session wires the **two highest-value remaining sources** and applies the table migration. **`react_error_boundary`** — both error boundaries in `apps/web/src/components/ErrorBoundary.tsx` (generic `ErrorBoundary` + always-mounted `GlobalErrorBoundary`) now call a shared `reportBoundaryError(error, info, boundary)` from `componentDidCatch`, emitting `source:'react_error_boundary'` with `context.boundary` + a 4000-char-capped `componentStack`. Because `GlobalErrorBoundary` mounts on every path incl. `/showcase/*`, the helper uses a **lazy `import('../lib/clientErrorLog.js')`** to keep the authed graph out of the showcase initial chunk ([[decisions/2026-05-21-atlas-showcase-bundle-split]]). **`unhandled_rejection`** — new `apps/web/src/lib/globalErrorHandlers.ts` (`installGlobalErrorHandlers()`) registers one idempotent `window.unhandledrejection` listener; it statically imports `clientErrorLog`, so it is imported **only from `bootAuthed.ts`** (authed-only — showcase ships no client-error telemetry). `window.onerror` deliberately out of scope (no matching enum source; React render errors already covered). **projectId resolver** — `clientErrorLog.ts` gains `setClientErrorProjectIdResolver(fn)`; `recordClientError` uses `input.projectId !== undefined ? input.projectId : safeResolveProjectId()` so an explicit value (incl. the persist helper's explicit `null`) wins, an omitted one falls back to the resolver (`bootAuthed.ts` registers `() => useProjectStore.getState().activeProjectId ?? null`); `safeResolveProjectId` swallows resolver throws. **Migration 039 applied to the LOCAL DEV DB** — investigation confirmed there is **no prod/staging DB** (staging parked, [[log/2026-04-21-staging-provisioning-decision-parked]]); only local dev Postgres exists, operator confirmed. Runner applies all pending in order (can't target one), so 039 + additive 040/041 (`CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS`, verified non-destructive) applied together via `node --env-file=.env --import=tsx src/db/migrate.ts`. Verified `client_error_events`: 14 cols, nullable `project_id`/`stack`, 2 indexes, 4-source CHECK constraint; `039` in `schema_migrations`. **Tests:** new `globalErrorHandlers.test.ts` (3) + `ErrorBoundary.telemetry.test.tsx` (3) + extended `clientErrorLog.test.ts` resolver block (3) — 20 targeted tests green; web tsc shows only the 3 pre-existing unrelated errors. Commit `2eb2aa6a` (frontend slice). **Remaining gap:** `api_client` is the last unwired source (deferred — lower value). ADR back-links: [[decisions/2026-05-21-atlas-showcase-bundle-split]], [[log/2026-05-21-client-error-telemetry-sink]].
- [2026-05-21 — Phase 5 (Slice B): Showcase observation loop](log/2026-05-21-atlas-phase-5-observation.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. The final phase of the Apricot-Lane-inspired Showcase Program — adds the observation loop the public `/showcase/three-streams` portal ([[log/2026-05-21-atlas-phase-3-showcase-portal]]) shipped without. Two blockers: the authed telemetry pipeline (`POST /api/v1/telemetry/act-interactions` + `act_interaction_events`) is `authenticate`-gated and its `user_id`/`project_id` are both NOT NULL — a cold showcase visitor is anonymous by definition. **Decision: a parallel anonymous-first path, not a relaxed authed one** ([[decisions/2026-05-21-atlas-showcase-observation-loop]]); the authed pipeline is left untouched. **Quantitative half** — migration `040_showcase_visitor_events.sql` (`bb54a4fb`) inverts the NOT-NULL invariants (nullable `user_id`/`project_id`; `session_id` the cross-event handle; `event_type` CHECK on 7 lifecycle events; `tier` CHECK NULL-or-enum; idempotent) + PUBLIC rate-limited (`60/min`) `POST /api/v1/telemetry/showcase-events` with best-effort `jwtVerify` (stamps `user_id` only if a bearer happens to be present) and best-effort per-event bulk insert (`cbe90535`). **Client wiring** (`57de13f8`) — `showcaseEventLog.ts` mirrors `actInteractionLog.ts`'s batcher shape but POSTs via plain `fetch` + `navigator.sendBeacon` with type-only `@ogden/shared` imports (keeps the Phase 3.5 lean SSG bundle free of `authStore`/`projectStore`/Cesium); instruments `TierChooser`/`ContactCTA`/route-mount/register/instantiate. **Qualitative half** — migration `041_showcase_feedback.sql` + PUBLIC `POST /api/v1/telemetry/showcase-feedback` + `FeedbackForm.tsx` mounted between `<ContactCTA>` and `<AttributionFooter>` (`051518e9`); `message` the one required field (client + route trim + DB CHECK backstop), `rating`/`contact` opt-in, reads (not creates) the telemetry `session_id` to cross-link, deliberately ungated by `VITE_ATLAS_TELEMETRY_ENABLED` (explicit submission is opt-in, not passive telemetry). **Covenant ratchet** (`f3a5aeb8`) — `covenant.test.ts`'s `git ls-files` subtree scan pulled both new files in scope automatically; one catch-and-fix where the `FeedbackForm` docstring *enumerated* the forbidden tokens and tripped the ratchet on its own prose (reworded). **Privacy posture:** anonymous by default (ephemeral `sessionStorage` id, no cookie/fingerprint/PII), the only PII channel (`showcase_feedback.contact`) is opt-in, cross-link not identity; consent banner deferred (documented in ADR). Gate: API tsc exit 0; web tsc 0 new errors above baseline; showcase vitest green incl. covenant ratchet + Apricot Lane exact-string. **Program complete** (Phase 0 → 5). ADR back-links: [[decisions/2026-05-21-atlas-showcase-observation-loop]], [[entities/showcase-portal]], [[log/2026-05-21-atlas-phase-2.5-livestock-seed]].

- [2026-05-21 — Phase G hotfix: Vite alias for `@ogden/shared/evidence`](log/2026-05-21-phase-g-vite-alias-hotfix.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Unblocks dev-server boot after Phase G G.1 added `./evidence` to `packages/shared/package.json` exports but did not update the parallel `resolve.alias` map in `apps/web/vite.config.ts`. Symptom: Vite v6.4.1 returned HTTP 500 on `DecisionTriad.tsx` / `LandVerdictCard.tsx` / `auditEmit.ts` with "Failed to resolve import `@ogden/shared/evidence`"; React root never mounted. Root cause: `vite.config.ts:172-196` carries an explicit alias map for every `@ogden/shared/*` subpath because Vite's dev-server cwd is `apps/web/` and cannot traverse up to the workspace-root node_modules; the bare `@ogden/shared` entry prefix-matched any unaliased subpath and rewrote it to `packages/shared/src/index.ts/evidence` (nonsense). Node's resolver was happy (verified via `require.resolve`); Vite's alias-first chain short-circuited before reaching the exports field. Fix: one-line add at `apps/web/vite.config.ts:194` — `'@ogden/shared/evidence': resolve(__dirname, '../../packages/shared/src/evidence/index.ts')` — placed before the bare-package fallback per the "more-specific first" rule in the surrounding comment. Verification: all three modules HTTP 200; `apps/web` typecheck clean for evidence code (3 pre-existing unrelated errors untouched: `StepBoundary.tsx`, `HostUnionContextMenu.test.tsx`, `HostUnionDrilldownCard.test.tsx`). Lesson: future subpath additions to `packages/shared/package.json` exports **must also** add the matching `vite.config.ts` alias entry — the two surfaces are parallel and Vite's prefix-match silently fails for any apps/web consumer otherwise.

- [2026-05-21 — Click-delete vertex fix (onMouseUp → onClick)](log/2026-05-21-click-delete-vertex-fix.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Bug-fix for user-reported "clicking on a vertex does not remove it" in real Chrome. Root cause: `clickDeleteDirectSelect.ts` attached deletion to `onMouseUp`, but MapboxDraw's `events.mouseup` routes click-gestures (`isClick`: ≤ 4 px / ≤ 500 ms) to `currentMode.onClick`, drag-releases to `currentMode.onMouseUp` — so plain vertex clicks never reached the delete branch. Two slices: **`90fef60a`** moved deletion to `onClick`, dropped the now-redundant in-mode pixel-threshold (MapboxDraw's own `isClick` already gates), and returns early without delegating to `stock.onClick` when the min-vertex guard fires (otherwise `clickActiveFeature` clears `selectedCoordPaths` and kicks the user out of vertex-edit on the 3rd vertex of a triangle); also resets `_cdVertexCoordPath` on every `onMouseDown`. **`16dc2d79`** appended a corrective "later" section to the [partial smoke-walk log](log/2026-05-21-observe-vertex-edit-and-click-delete.md) striking through its "harness limitation" framing — the harness was a red herring layered on top of a real regression. Typecheck exit 0. Real-browser keystroke confirmation of the remaining smoke-walk steps still owed. Branch hygiene: stashed unrelated parallel-session edits (basemap-water-adoption + template_slug migration) before commit, restored after push; `git fetch` 2/0 before push; FF clean.

- [2026-05-21 — Observe-anno "stuck source" diagnosis closed as headless-RAF artefact](log/2026-05-21-observe-anno-sources-false-alarm.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. **No code change.** Wiki-only documentation closing the "four observe-anno sources never reach `loaded:true`" investigation as not-a-bug. Live preview verification at `/v3/project/mtc/observe` with two seeded Conventional Crop polygons shows `m.isSourceLoaded('observe-anno-conventional-crop') === true` and `queryRenderedFeatures` returning the crop with correct `annoKind`/`annoId` props — after exactly one `_render()` tick. The prior session's "render loop is dead" conclusion was a property-name miss: it probed `m._frame`, but MapLibre 5.x renamed that field to `_frameRequest` and now schedules frames via `AbortController` + `browser.frameAsync` ([`node_modules/maplibre-gl/dist/maplibre-gl-dev.js:57944`](../node_modules/maplibre-gl/dist/maplibre-gl-dev.js)). Re-probing the correct field shows a frame IS queued — it just never resolves while the Claude Preview tab is backgrounded (headless Chrome throttles RAF for inactive tabs). All geojson sources show the same idle-paused profile in the preview (`be-v2-*`, `matrix-*-dem`, `design-el-extrusion`, `diagnose-parcel-boundary`), not just the named four; the "siblings load normally" framing in the brief was a probe-timing artefact. **Diagnostic technique worth keeping:** when debugging "isSourceLoaded never true" under Claude Preview, force a paint via `m._render(performance.now())` from the eval console to drain `_updatedSources` and resume paused SourceCaches synchronously enough to read a real state. **Implication for the [vertex-edit + click-delete smoke walk](log/2026-05-21-observe-vertex-edit-and-click-delete.md):** if "clicks don't open detail panels" reproduces in a real browser, the cause is not stuck sources — likelier suspects are `SelectionFloater` consuming the click before the layer handler, the 50 ms `consumedAt` deduper in `ObserveAnnotationLayers.tsx` mis-rejecting, or the form store's `existingId === id && kind === kind` early-return. Disposition: closed as not-a-bug; future sessions should re-test in a real browser before re-opening this thread.

Vegetation + pasture now describe the ground-cover *matrix*; crops + buildings sit on top as opaque *patches* rather than translucent blends. Four phases in one slice: (1) `conventionalCrop` fill-opacity 0.22 → 0.55 and `building` 0.35 → 0.6 in `ObserveAnnotationLayers.tsx` so patches occlude the matrix underneath (layer-order already correct). MapLibre fill/line layers handle MultiPolygon natively, no paint change. (4) New **"Fill remainder (subtract crops & buildings)"** checkbox in `VegetationTool` and `PastureTool` popovers — when on, `place(boundary)` runs `subtractPatches`: reduce `turf.difference(turf.featureCollection([acc, turf.feature(g)]))` over crops ∪ buildings; `null` result (boundary fully covered) bails with a `console.info` and skips creation, otherwise the Polygon/MultiPolygon flows through the existing `createWithDefaults() → form → addPatch()` path. Two commits — round 1 `14db482f` adds an "Edit vertices" button to `AnnotationDetailPanel` (gated on `POLYGON_KINDS.has(kind) || LINESTRING_KINDS.has(kind)`; sector arcs and point kinds excluded), routing through `observeSelectionStore.set([{kind,id}]) + setMoveMode(true) + closeStore()` (NOT the local `close` wrapper — that clears selection) so the existing `AnnotationVertexEditHandler` path picks up. `conventionalCrop` and `pasture` registered in `POLYGON_KINDS` of `annotationGeometryRegistry` with new `readPolygon` / `writePolygon` cases routing to `useConventionalCropStore.updateConventionalCrop({ geometry })` + `usePastureStore.updatePasture({ geometry })`. Silent refusal per user choice — no toast. `SharedVertexEditHandler.tsx` registers the mode on the per-mount `MapboxDraw` instance and switches `changeMode` from `'direct_select'` to `CLICK_DELETE_DIRECT_SELECT`; Plan-stage `PlanVertexEditHandler` inherits for free via composition. **Behaviour.** Click vertex (no drag) → vertex deleted; click+drag → moves (unchanged); midpoint click → adds vertex (unchanged); click vertex on triangle / 2-vertex line → nothing (silently gated); Esc → exits vertex-edit (unchanged); Cmd-Z → restores via store `temporal()` middleware. `draw_polygon` mode for new polygons unaffected. **Verification.** `pnpm --filter @ogden/web typecheck` shows only 3 pre-existing unrelated errors (`StepBoundary.tsx:365`, two `HostUnion…` test files) — none in touched files. - [2026-05-30 — B4 tooltip multi-pin (Slice L)](log/2026-05-30-b4-tooltip-multi-pin.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes Slice L of the B4 tooltip remaining-deferrals roadmap. Retires the 2026-05-26 single-pin invariant: `pinnedUnion` (single `{ point, entries, hostIds }` object) replaced with `pinnedHosts: Map<string, HostBlock>` keyed by hostId; per-host click toggle, ESC + tap-outside clear ALL pins, single cursor-anchored stack merging pinned (insertion order, `pinned: true`) with hover (filtered by `!pinnedHosts.has`, `pinned: false`). `lastCursorPointRef` freezes the anchor when the cursor leaves canvas with pins active. Gold accent moves from container-level `.tooltip[data-pinned='true']` (border-color) to per-block `.hostBlock[data-pinned='true']` (2px gold left-border + 6px padding-left) so mixed pinned + hover stacks distinguish sticky from hover-along blocks at a glance. `HostBlockEntry` gains `pinned: boolean` (kept off `HostBlockProps` so the raw-data interface stays narrow); scroll-cap derivation moves from `!!pinned` to `entries.some(e => e.pinned)`. `sameHostIdSet()` helper deleted. **Use-case justification.** Roadmap required "design conversation about whether the use case (steward wanting to compare 2+ hosts side-by-side) is real before committing." Consulted **Permaculture Scholar NotebookLM (`5aa3dcf3-…`)** — unequivocal yes, citing four canonical permaculture design flows requiring simultaneous comparison of overlapping host canopies: (1) **50-year mature-canopy simulation** (spacing for tree A depends on B/C/D's mature spreads in the same frame); (2) **Edge maximization** (Holmgren P11 "Use Edges and Value the Marginal" — biodiversity concentrates in spaces *between* canopies; productive edge can't be designed one tree at a time); (3) **Cross-guild ecological aggregation** (N-fixers + dynamic accumulators + insectaries aggregate into coverage or redundancy — multi-guild question by definition); (4) **Suntrap / microclimate engineering** (U-shape / horseshoe arrangements creating sheltered microclimates — aggregate footprint + continuous shadow evaluated as a unit). Holmgren P8 ("Integrate Rather Than Segregate") underwrites all four. Single-pin was a segregation affordance working against P8. Scholar citations degenerate (~290 references to same handful of snippets — known indexer artifact); substantive claims hold independently against any permaculture-design textbook. **Key architectural choices.** `Map<hostId, HostBlock>` for O(1) per-host toggle + insertion-order iteration (newly-pinned at top of pinned section, consistent with 2026-05-27 topmost-first convention). Per-block accent not container-level so mixed stacks communicate sticky vs hover-along visually. `pinned` on `HostBlockEntry` not `HostBlockProps` (display-state, not raw-data payload). Single cursor-anchored stack rather than separate portals per pin (matches "these are the hosts I'm comparing" mental model). ESC + tap-outside clear ALL pins per roadmap recommendation ("get this off my screen" rarely scoped to one host). In-tooltip dismiss button OUT OF SCOPE — below Slice K's threshold=4 the tooltip is `pointer-events: none`, can't receive clicks without retiring the 2026-05-25 invariant; Slice M's drill-down surface (interactive by design) can ship it. **Tests.** Migrated test #3 from container-level `pinned` prop to per-entry; scroll-cap tests migrated to entry-level `pinned: true`. New `describe('multi-pin (Slice L)', ...)` with four cases: mixed pinned + hover (only pinned blocks carry data-pinned; root never carries data-pinned), all-pinned stack (every block carries data-pinned; separators between), all-hover stack (no data-pinned anywhere), scrollable regression guard (1 pinned + 3 hover = 4 ≥ threshold ⇒ scrollable because `entries.some` predicate, guarding against future tightening to "all pinned"). **Verification.** `npx vitest run src/v3/plan/layers` → 28/28 (24 prior + 4 new). `npx vitest run src/v3/plan src/features/agroforestry` → 288/288 (36 files; +4 over Slice N's 284). `npx tsc --noEmit` clean on touched files; pre-existing unrelated errors elsewhere unchanged. Preview-server visual check not possible in this worktree (Vite resolves against worktree-root `node_modules` which doesn't exist) — stated explicitly per project CLAUDE.md "say so rather than assuming success." **Invariants preserved.** Slice K scroll-cap carve-out + tooltip-testid tap-outside exemption; Slice J / I / H; 2026-05-25 `pointer-events: none` in hover mode + pinned-small-stack; 2026-05-27 multi-feature fan-out (each feature toggles independently); 2026-05-28 ESC + tap-outside dismiss (semantics flip from "clear one" to "clear all"); 2026-05-29 / 30 fade machinery (`pinned` rides alongside `phase`); 2026-05-30 Slice N i18n seam (no new strings). **Invariant retired.** 2026-05-26 single-pin explicitly rolled back; ADR remains in wiki as historical context (defensive reasoning correct at the time, design question now answered). **Out of scope.** In-tooltip dismiss button (Slice M's space); pinned-count badge ("📌 N" header indicator — additive, defer); per-guild breakdown line inside a block (Slice O rejection deferred this to Slice M); persistence across page reloads (transient UI); keyboard navigation between pinned blocks (accessibility pass); integration tests for `PlanDataLayers` click-toggle Map logic (defer until a regression points at it). Roadmap status: H + I + J + K + N + O + L shipped. **Remaining: Slice M** (hover-card drill-down — per-block click opens a richer surface listing per-guild breakdowns; depends on L's per-block addressability, which now exists).
- [2026-05-30 — B4 per-layer tinted stripe rejection (Slice O — second pass)](log/2026-05-30-b4-tooltip-per-layer-stripe-rejection.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes Slice O of the B4 tooltip remaining-deferrals roadmap as a **documentation-only rejection** — no code change. The roadmap was explicit that this slice "must start with a research/decision step … decide whether the stripe is genuinely distinguishable (different surface) or re-introduces the same problem (same concept, different shape). Only then design the implementation, or document the second rejection with fresh reasoning." This slice ships the second-rejection path. **Prior rejections recap.** 2026-05-24 halo viz ADR colored the union halo neutral grey, explicitly rejecting `LAYER_TINT`: *"Neutral grey (not LAYER_TINT) because the union is a per-host aggregate, not a per-layer geometry; layer-tinting would mislead the eye into reading the halo as canopy-layer-specific."* 2026-05-25 hover tooltip ADR carried the reasoning forward to the tooltip stripe: *"the union is a per-host aggregate; layer-tinting would reintroduce the misleading-hue concern 2026-05-24 called out for the halo itself."* Both deferred as "revisit if needed." **Fresh counter-argument considered.** The natural revisit: the halo is on the map (color = layer-data), but the tooltip is a *separate UI surface* with its own visual conventions (already carries a gold "saved overlap" accent — a non-data color), so a stripe there would read as "category metadata," not as "this geometry = green-layer." **Why the counter-argument fails on two grounds.** (1) **Visual contiguity.** The tooltip is cursor-anchored adjacent to the halo it describes — stewards see them simultaneously. A green stripe next to a grey halo invites the eye to bind "this host = green," propagating the layer-tint association from the *label* onto the halo it labels. The surface boundary doesn't exist for the eye when the surfaces are positionally adjacent; the 2026-05-24 reasoning survives unchanged: the stripe tints the halo's label, which is the same problem one frame downstream. (2) **"Dominant" is the wrong reduction.** A host is in the silvopasture data because it carries *multiple* canopy layers (polyculture by construction). Every available definition of "dominant" elevates one layer above the others — biggest area biases toward fast-spreading shrubs, most members biases toward groundcovers, tallest requires schema work (data model doesn't track per-member heights), alphabetical is arbitrary and defensible only as a tie-breaker. Polyculture composition is the load-bearing feature of the model; hiding four-fifths of it behind one layer's color is a model violation, not a presentation choice. **What the steward actually needs (and where it goes).** The existing counts line — *"3 guilds · 7 canopy-bearing members"* — already surfaces polyculture composition. If at-a-glance per-layer breakdown matters, the right UI is a small list inside the tooltip (e.g. `overstory ×2 · midstory ×3 · understory ×2`), with each layer name in its own tint *as a label, not as a category color for the host as a whole*. **This breakdown is not in scope for Slice O** — it overlaps with **Slice M** (hover-card drill-down), where the natural design move is to expand a block into a richer surface that lists per-guild breakdowns. Whoever picks Slice M up next can lean on this ADR's reasoning to justify the breakdown approach. **Status flip.** 2026-05-24 / 25 ADRs left this as "deferred — revisit if needed." This slice flips it to **decided rejection**. Future roadmap sweeps should not re-list it as candidate work without the underlying constraint (silvopasture is polyculture-by-construction; "dominant layer" is information loss) materially changing. **Out of scope.** Code changes (none, by design); per-guild breakdown line in the tooltip text (Slice M's space); layer-aware *icons* on the tooltip (canopy/midstory/understory glyphs — distinct from color-tint, worth a separate design conversation); changes to the existing `LAYER_TINT` palette on the map's per-member geometries (those remain correct — per-member geometries genuinely belong to a single layer); light/dark theming (separate deferral). **Verification.** No code change → no tests to run, no tsc to check, no preview-server to verify. The slice's deliverable is this log entry + the ADR; both are reviewable in `git log`. **Invariants preserved.** Every B4 invariant from earlier ADRs holds verbatim — no surface has been touched. Roadmap status: H + I + J + K + N shipped as code; **O shipped as a documented rejection**. Remaining: **Slice L** (multi-pin — substantial slice; needs design conversation about whether the "steward wants to compare 2+ hosts side-by-side" use case is real before committing) and **Slice M** (hover-card drill-down — depends on L's per-block addressability).
- [2026-05-30 — B4 tooltip i18n seam (Slice N)](log/2026-05-30-b4-tooltip-i18n-seam.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes Slice N of the B4 tooltip remaining-deferrals roadmap by shipping the small-path option (path 2): extracts every English string the tooltip surfaces into a new colocated `tooltipStrings.ts` module with a clean seam for future i18next adoption, **without** bootstrapping i18next project-wide. **What changed.** New `apps/web/src/v3/plan/layers/tooltipStrings.ts`: `tooltipStrings` const object holds 3 row labels (`unionFootprint` = "Union footprint", `rawDiskSum` = "Raw π·r² sum", `savedOverlap` = "Saved overlap"); two formatter functions encapsulate the unit-suffix + pluralization logic — `formatAreaM2(n)` rounds + appends " m²", `formatHostCounts(guildCount, memberCount)` renders the counts line with English n===1 binary pluralization ("guild"/"guilds", "member"/"members"), the " · " separator, and the "canopy-bearing" qualifier all baked in. `HostCanopyUnionTooltip.tsx` removes its inline `formatM2` helper, imports the three exports, swaps inline ternaries for the formatter call, and replaces bare string literals with `{tooltipStrings.unionFootprint}` etc. 6 formatter unit tests pin area rounding (incl. 0.49 → "0 m²" toward-zero edge) + plural/singular/zero-as-plural combinations. **Why path 2 not path 1.** `react-i18next` + `i18next` are deps but **zero** `useTranslation` / `i18n.init` call sites exist anywhere in `apps/web/src` — the tooltip would be the first consumer. Path 1 would force five ADR-worthy decisions in this slice's scope: bootstrap location, `<I18nextProvider>` wrapper near the app root (startup-time + pending Atlas-portal SSR consideration), resource-file layout (namespace boundaries), bundle-size assessment (~30kB gzipped naively bundled), and a project-wide copy-migration policy. The constants module gets the strings *organised* without forcing any of those bets; path 1 stays available as a follow-up when a second locale is confirmed. **Why a TS module, not a JSON resource file.** JSON is standard i18next layout but can't hold the formatter functions — splitting them now would leave a half-organised seam. When i18next lands, formatters become a thin shim around `t()` and the string-constant object migrates to JSON; the file shrinks or disappears. **Why keep English n===1 in-module.** A real i18n library will replace it with CLDR plural rules per locale (Arabic: six forms; Russian: three). Current formatter signature `(count, count) => string` is narrow on purpose — future swap to `t('tooltip.hostCounts', { guildCount, memberCount })` requires no call-site changes. **Migration recipe documented** in the module header docstring: (1) add `apps/web/src/i18n/index.ts` i18next bootstrap, (2) wrap `<App />` in `<I18nextProvider>`, (3) swap `tooltipStrings.foo` for `t('tooltip.foo')`, (4) move values into `locales/en/tooltip.json`, (5) delete the module. **Strings preserved byte-identically.** Row labels, " m²" suffix, " · " separator, "canopy-bearing" qualifier, n===1 binary pluralization — all unchanged. The existing tooltip rendering tests pass without modification, strong evidence the refactor changed nothing observable. **Verification.** `npx vitest run src/v3/plan/layers` → 24/24 (12 tooltip + 6 memberDragMath + 6 new tooltipStrings); `npx vitest run src/v3/plan src/features/agroforestry` → 284/284 (36 files; +6 over Slice K); `npx tsc --noEmit` clean on touched files; preview-server visual check not possible in this worktree per project CLAUDE.md "say so rather than assuming success" — refactor is a pure extraction whose visible output is byte-identical per the unchanged rendering tests. **Invariants preserved.** All Slice K (scroll-cap carve-out, data-scrollable threshold=4), J / I / H, and earlier B4 invariants (mouseleave-driven dismiss in hover mode + small-pinned, single-pin, multi-feature fan-out, touch tap-outside dismiss, enter + exit + per-block + reverse-in-flight fade, `prefers-reduced-motion`). **Out of scope.** Bootstrapping i18next (path 1, deferred); extracting strings from any other surface (tooltip-only by scope); number formatting beyond m² (decimal separators, grouping — available once i18next lands); RTL layout (separate infrastructure decision — CSS logical properties + `[dir]` attribute on `<html>`). Roadmap status: H + I + J + K + N shipped; next is **Slice O** (per-layer tinted accent stripe — research/decision step first, may ship as a "still rejected" ADR rather than code) per the approved execution order.
- [2026-05-30 — B4 tooltip max-height scroll cap (Slice K)](log/2026-05-30-b4-tooltip-scroll-cap.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes Slice K of the B4 tooltip remaining-deferrals roadmap — the highest-risk wave-C entry because **any** scroll affordance on the host-canopy-union tooltip requires `pointer-events: auto`, which collides with the 2026-05-25 invariant that the tooltip must NEVER steal the underlying union layer's mouseleave. **The carve-out.** `.tooltip[data-scrollable='true']` activates only when `pinned=true AND entries.length >= 4`. The CSS rule adds `max-height: calc(100vh - 80px)`, `overflow-y: auto`, and `pointer-events: auto`. Below either condition the invariant survives verbatim: hover mode + any host count = `pointer-events: none` and mouseleave-driven dismiss; pinned + 1–3 hosts = same. Above both conditions, mouseleave is moot — when pinned, dismissal is via ESC, click-again-on-host, or tap-outside-canvas-and-outside-tooltip, none of which depend on the tooltip's pointer-events. **Tap-outside handler carve-out (PlanDataLayers).** `onDocPointerDown` would have dismissed pointerdowns on the tooltip's scrollbar/content (target not in canvas → fall through). New early-return: `if (target instanceof Element && target.closest('[data-testid="host-canopy-union-tooltip"]')) return;`. The tooltip is portalled to the document body so PlanDataLayers can't hold a ref to it — the data-testid already used by tests becomes the production query selector, no portal-aware ref forwarding needed. **Edge-clamp adjustment.** Raw `entries.length * PER_BLOCK_H` would over-reserve vertical space when the surface is scroll-capped (e.g. 20-host pinned stack) and push the anchor unnecessarily high; new `scrollCapMaxH = Math.max(PER_BLOCK_H, viewportH - 80)` bounds the estimatedH when `scrollable`. `Math.max(PER_BLOCK_H, ...)` guards against pathologically short viewports. **Threshold = 4.** Three hosts (~340px) fits 768px viewport comfortably; four (~448px) tight; five+ clips. Single `SCROLL_CAP_THRESHOLD = 4` module constant so a future tuning round can move it without touching consumers. **Reserve = 80px.** `calc(100vh - 80px)` matches the existing edge-clamp's intuitive budget (12px cursor gap + 8px padding at top/bottom + DesignToolRail headroom); on a 720px viewport ~640px usable ≈ 5.9 blocks, "scroll if you must" not "scroll constantly." **Why not WAAPI / wheel-capture.** The roadmap's alternative — capture `wheel` events on the document, translate to a CSS-variable offset on a virtual scrollable container — would preserve the 2026-05-25 invariant verbatim but re-implement overscroll, inertia, scrollbar-drag, keyboard scroll, and require a separate `touchmove` path for tablets. The dual carve-out (CSS + tap-outside) ships in ~10 lines and inherits every native scroll affordance for free; the narrow carve-out window keeps the invariant holding in every state the steward meets during normal hover flow. **Why threshold-by-entry-count not viewport-bound.** The cleaner predicate would be `scrollable = pinned && rawEstimatedH > scrollCapMaxH`, but (a) entries.length is stable across viewport changes (resize doesn't toggle the carve-out under a pinned steward) and (b) the test surface stays simpler. If the fixed threshold proves wrong for small viewports, swap the predicate without changing the data-attribute contract. **Reused, not built:** existing portal mount; existing data-testid; existing tap-outside listener; existing edge-clamp logic; existing fade machinery (data-visible / data-exiting / transition tokens). **Tests added:** 4 under `scroll-cap carve-out (Slice K)` describe — below-threshold pinned = no data-scrollable; above-threshold unpinned = no data-scrollable (hover invariant survives); at-threshold pinned = data-scrollable='true'; very-tall (20-host) pinned at viewport-top = data-scrollable='true' + edge-clamp produces non-negative top (regression guard). **Verification:** `npx vitest run src/v3/plan/layers/__tests__/HostCanopyUnionTooltip.test.tsx` → 12/12 (8 prior + 4 new); `npx vitest run src/v3/plan src/features/agroforestry` → 278/278 (35 files; +4 over Slice J); `npx tsc --noEmit` clean on the three touched files (pre-existing unrelated errors elsewhere unchanged); preview-server visual check not possible in this worktree per project CLAUDE.md "say so rather than assuming success" — data-attribute contract fully unit-test-covered, visible scroll relies on browser-native `overflow-y: auto`. **Invariants preserved:** 2026-05-25 (mouseleave-driven dismiss in hover mode + pinned-small-stack), 2026-05-26 (single-pin), 2026-05-27 (multi-feature fan-out), 2026-05-28 (touch tap-outside dismiss), 2026-05-29 + 30 (enter + exit + per-block + reverse-in-flight fade), `prefers-reduced-motion`. **Out of scope:** Slice L multi-pin (separate slice; depends on this one), Slice M hover-card drill-down (depends on L), viewport-aware predicate, sticky block headers when scrolling, keyboard arrow-key navigation between blocks. Roadmap status: H + I + J + K shipped; next is **Slice N** (tooltip i18n small path) per the approved execution order.
- [2026-05-30 — B4 InlineFeaturePopover exit fade (Slice J)](log/2026-05-30-b4-inline-popover-exit-fade.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes Slice J of the B4 tooltip remaining-deferrals roadmap, consuming the `--motion-overlay-*` tokens added in Slice I. Click-driven inline mini-form `InlineFeaturePopover` adopts the same deferred-unmount machinery the 2026-05-30 host-canopy-union tooltip ship landed: a `displayed: InlineFormPayload | null` mirror state lives one exit-transition longer than `useInlineFormStore.active`, `exiting: boolean` flips at the same time `active` goes null, `visible: boolean` flips via `useLayoutEffect` after mount so the enter transition fires from `opacity: 0`/`translateY(2px)` → `opacity: 1`/`translateY(0)`. CSS-Module `.popover` rule gains the from-state + `transition: opacity var(--motion-overlay-duration) var(--motion-overlay-ease-out), transform var(--motion-overlay-duration) var(--motion-overlay-ease-out)`. New `.popover[data-visible='true']` selector targets the visible state; new `.popover[data-exiting='true']` mirrors the from-state, switches the easing token to `--motion-overlay-ease-in`, and adds **`pointer-events: none`** so a mid-fade click on a fading Save/Cancel button is physically impossible. `prefers-reduced-motion: reduce` block nulls both transitions so reduced-motion users see instant dismissal. **The interactivity invariant difference from the tooltip.** Tooltip is `pointer-events: none` — invariant: "must never steal events from the underlying layer." Popover is `pointer-events: auto` — owns inputs, Save, Cancel, custom actions. So the tooltip's invariant doesn't transfer. New invariant: **a mid-fade click on a fading button must not race the displayed-mirror cleanup.** Defense-in-depth: exit-state CSS drops `pointer-events: none` (primary defence), Save/Cancel handlers also guard on `if (!active)` (free insurance — store entry has cleared by the time exit starts). **Value-reset block now skips active=null.** Pre-fade logic unconditionally cleared `values` when `active` went null; with deferred unmount the form renders through the fade and clearing values mid-fade would visually empty every input. New logic only resets when active becomes a **new non-null payload**; active going null is the exit signal and values stay frozen until `displayed` clears. **`onPopoverTransitionEnd` filters on three conditions.** `propertyName === 'opacity'` (rejects the transform-property transitionend so the unmount is deterministic and tied to the visually-disappearing property), `target === currentTarget` (rejects bubbled child transitionends from nested `<input>`, `<select>`, `<button>` focus-ring + hover-state transitions), `exiting === true` (rejects post-reverse-in-flight transitionends that would spuriously unmount a restored form). 200ms safety `setTimeout` covers `prefers-reduced-motion` where transitionend never fires. **Render guard switched from `if (!active) return null` → `if (!displayed) return null`** so the form stays mounted through the fade; title, fields, customActions iteration all read from `displayed`. New 4-test suite `InlineFeaturePopover.test.tsx` pins: cold-start renders nothing; `open()` mounts with `data-visible='true'`; `close()` flips `data-exiting='true'`, transform-property transitionend does NOT unmount but opacity-property transitionend does; reverse-in-flight `open()` during exit restores form and subsequent opacity transitionend does not spuriously unmount. Uses the same `fireTransitionEnd(el, propertyName)` `Object.defineProperty` happy-dom helper as the 2026-05-30 tooltip tests. **Reused, not built:** Slice I `--motion-overlay-*` tokens; deferred-unmount pattern from the 2026-05-30 tooltip ship; existing ESC + click-outside listeners (still gated on `active` so they auto-detach at exit start — correct, because the form is no longer interactive). **Invariants preserved:** schema-driven render (title, fields, customActions, required-field gate, disclosure expansion) unchanged; ESC + click-outside dismiss; reduced-motion behaviour. **Out of scope:** the slide-up dialog used for written reports (different surface class — slide-up animation, not fade); cubic-bezier alignment of overlay surfaces with the project's `--ease-out`/`--ease-in` family (deferred per the Slice I ADR; revisit when a third consumer arrives); per-field exit animations within the popover. **Verification:** `npx vitest run src/v3/plan src/features/agroforestry` → 274/274 green (35 files; +4 new InlineFeaturePopover tests; 8/8 tooltip tests untouched); `npx tsc --noEmit` clean on touched files (pre-existing unrelated errors in `LandAssessmentSlideUp.tsx`, `AtlasAIPanel.tsx`, `HydrologyRightPanel.tsx` confirmed unchanged via baseline grep); preview-server visual check not possible in this worktree (Vite resolves against worktree-root `node_modules` which doesn't exist) — stated explicitly per project CLAUDE.md "say so rather than assuming success," structurally identical to the 2026-05-30 tooltip ship whose contract is fully unit-test-covered. Roadmap status: H + I + J shipped; next is **Slice K** (max-height scroll cap when N hosts is large) which carries the `pointer-events` carve-out risk.
- [2026-05-30 — B4 motion-token harmonisation (Slice I)](log/2026-05-30-b4-motion-token-harmonisation.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes Slice I of the B4 tooltip remaining-deferrals roadmap. Extracts the four hard-coded overlay-fade literals from `HostCanopyUnionTooltip.module.css` (duration `120ms`, translate `2px`, easing `ease-out`/`ease-in`) into a new `--motion-overlay-*` token family declared on `:root` in [apps/web/src/styles/tokens.css](../apps/web/src/styles/tokens.css) alongside the existing `--duration-*` / `--ease-*` families. Four sites of `transition: opacity 120ms ease-... , transform 120ms ease-...` rewritten as `var(...)` calls; three `translateY(2px)` sites likewise. `prefers-reduced-motion: reduce` block unchanged (nulls `transition` entirely, no per-token override needed). **Why a new family, not reuse `--duration-*` / `--ease-*`.** Existing duration ladder is 100/200/400/600ms; tooltip's 120ms was tuned because 100ms felt snappy and 200ms felt draggy under cursor motion. Existing `--ease-out`/`--ease-in` are cubic-beziers (`cubic-bezier(0, 0, 0.2, 1)` / `cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 1, 1)`); tooltip ships with bare CSS keywords (`cubic-bezier(0, 0, 0.58, 1)` / `cubic-bezier(0.42, 0, 1, 1)`). Coercing to either would ship a visual change as part of a "token extraction" slice. New family preserves literals verbatim; cubic-bezier alignment deferred to a follow-up ADR after Slice J's adoption verifies the current curves feel right with two consumers. **Why CSS custom properties, not TS constants.** CSS Modules can't reference TS without inline `style={{}}` (loses scoping) or a CSS-in-JS pipeline (overkill for four literals). The 200ms safety timeout in `PlanDataLayers.tsx` does duplicate `--motion-overlay-duration + slack`, but the slack is the load-bearing part — if a second JS consumer materialises we'll revisit. **Why these four tokens specifically.** Two easings (not one) because enter accelerates toward the visible state and exit decelerates away from it; CSS variables can't carry direction. One duration (not three) because the 2026-05-30 ship uses 120ms across enter / exit / reverse-in-flight — different durations per intent would be a design change, not extraction. **Tokens.css is already imported once at the app root via [app/index.css:6](../apps/web/src/app/index.css), so no additional wiring needed and CSS custom properties propagate through the cascade into CSS-Modules-scoped class names.** Tests untouched — contract tests only assert data-attrs + event handling, neither affected by value extraction. 8/8 tooltip + 63/63 agroforestry green. Touched files TS-clean. **Unlocks Slice J** (InlineFeaturePopover exit fade) which can adopt the same tokens at birth so the two map-overlay surfaces fade in sync. Roadmap deferrals: cubic-bezier alignment, dark-mode-only overrides, additional surface-class families (`--motion-modal-*` etc) all kept deferred.
