- [2026-05-30 — B4 follow-up: per-block tooltip fade + reverse-in-flight](log/2026-05-30-b4-tooltip-perblock-fade-and-reverse.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes the last two still-deferred bullets from the 2026-05-29 exit-fade ADR: per-block exit fade in multi-host stacks, and reverse-in-flight animation when `activeUnion` returns non-null mid-exit. Fade machinery refactored from CSS keyframes (`@keyframes tooltipFadeIn` / `tooltipFadeOut`) to **CSS transitions** on opacity + transform; `.tooltip` mounts at `opacity: 0` and `.tooltip[data-visible='true']` flips to `opacity: 1` (the enter transition fires from a `useLayoutEffect` that sets `visible=true` on mount); `.tooltip[data-exiting='true']` takes opacity back to 0 with `ease-in` timing. New `.hostBlock` rule mirrors the same shape for per-block fades. `prefers-reduced-motion: reduce` override nulls all four selectors' `transition`. **Reverse-in-flight is free** with transitions: removing `data-exiting` mid-fade lets the transition interpolate from the current visible value back to 1, with no snap and no JS — making the 2026-05-29 monotonic-key remount pattern unnecessary. `HostCanopyUnionTooltip.tsx` exports a new `HostBlockEntry` interface (hostId + per-entry `phase: 'entering' | 'exiting'`); `HostBlock` renders `data-testid='host-block-${hostId}'`, `data-exiting='true'` when phase==='exiting', and an `onTransitionEnd` filtered by `propertyName==='opacity'` + `target===currentTarget` that fires a new `onEntryExited?: (hostId: string) => void` prop. Container's own `onTransitionEnd` filters by both `propertyName==='opacity'` and `target===currentTarget` so bubbled per-block transitionends don't fire `onExited`. **Merge-by-hostId.** `PlanDataLayers.displayedUnion` state shape replaces 2026-05-29's `key + entries: HostBlock[]` with per-entry phase tracking (`entries: HostBlockEntry[]`); the monotonic key is gone. The mirror `useEffect` rewrites the merge: kept hosts (in both old and new sets) carry forward with phase `entering` and refreshed data; dropped hosts (in old but not new) flip to phase `exiting` and stay in the array; new hosts are appended in MapLibre topmost-first order. The React `key` on the rendered map iterator is now `entry.hostId` (stable per host) so a block's in-flight transition isn't cancelled when siblings drop out and the array re-indexes. `onEntryExited` callback drops the hostId from the entries array — or clears the mirror entirely if the last block just finished fading. Safety timeout bumped 180 → 200 ms (120 ms transition + 80 ms slack to absorb event-loop jitter and the `prefers-reduced-motion` instant-change case where transitionend doesn't fire). **Test scaffolding.** New `fireTransitionEnd(el, propertyName)` helper — `@testing-library/dom`'s `createEvent.transitionEnd` passes init to the constructor without a fallback, and happy-dom's `TransitionEvent` constructor silently drops the `propertyName` init key, so the helper `Object.defineProperty`'s the value onto the event post-construction. Existing tests migrated from `fireEvent.animationEnd({ animationName: 'tooltipFadeOut' })` to the new helper. Two new tests: reverse-in-flight asserts that flipping `exiting` from true → false during re-render clears `data-exiting` and a subsequent opacity transitionend does NOT fire `onExited`; per-block exit asserts that an entry with `phase='exiting'` carries `data-exiting='true'`, that opacity transitionend fires `onEntryExited(hostId)`, and that sibling `entering` blocks + transform-property transitionends do not. **Why transitions, not WAAPI.** The 2026-05-29 ADR speculated about `element.animate()` + `animation.reverse()`. Transitions get the same behaviour with zero JS: they always interpolate from the current computed value, which is exactly what "reverse" means for a single-property fade. **Why merge by hostId.** When the active set shrinks, the dropped host has to stay in the displayed array long enough to fade; indices shift under set changes, so a key-by-index would cancel its transition when the array re-reconciled. Invariants preserved: `pointer-events: none`, single-pin model, ESC + tap-outside-to-dismiss, multi-feature fan-out (2026-05-27), edge-clamp + entries-aware `ESTIMATED_H` (counts every block including phase-`exiting` ones so a tooltip about to lose a block stays clamped conservatively — no flicker-reposition mid-fade), reduced-motion behaviour (was: no keyframe animation; now: no transition). 71/71 vitest green (8 tooltip + 63 agroforestry; +2 tooltip tests over the 2026-05-29 ship). Touched files TS-clean. 2026-05-29 ADR reverse-in-flight + per-block bullets flipped open → closed.
- [2026-05-21 — Phase D: J-curve + SOM trajectory + covenant rename](log/2026-05-21-phase-d-jcurve-and-som-trajectory.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Seven per-sub-phase commits closing the Apricot-Lane Phase D boundary (Feasibility / J-Curve + longitudinal SOM + residual covenant rename across Capital Partner + Scenario Comparison surfaces): **D.1** (`31938a4c`) lands `apps/web/src/features/financial/engine/transitionBudget.ts` — pure aggregation `computeTransitionBudget(cashflow)` over the existing `computeCashflow` output emitting `TransitionYear[]` with a 3-band phase label (`establishment` 0–2 / `build-up` 3–5 / `maturation` 6+) + `jCurveTrough()` returning `{ troughYear, troughValue, breakevenYear }`; - [2026-05-21 — fix(web): Vite dev proxy translates ECONNREFUSED into API_OFFLINE envelope](log/2026-05-21-vite-proxy-api-offline-envelope.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes the "Response not JSON (500)" papercut on `POST /api/v1/auth/register` from `http://localhost:5200/login`. Confirmed via `Test-NetConnection` + direct `/health` probe that nothing was listening on port 3001; the 500 was Vite's dev proxy returning plain-text HTML for `ECONNREFUSED`, not the API (whose global `setErrorHandler` in `apps/api/src/app.ts` *always* sends a JSON envelope, so a non-JSON 500 cannot originate there). Added `configure` + `proxy.on('error', …)` to the `/api` entry in `apps/web/vite.config.ts` that emits a `503` carrying the API's own envelope shape `{ data: null, error: { code: 'API_OFFLINE', message: "API server unreachable at http://localhost:3001 (<errno>). Start it with:  pnpm --filter @ogden/api dev" } }`. `apiClient.ts` flows the envelope through unchanged → LoginPage `role="alert"` banner renders the actionable instruction verbatim. Iterated once on the message format — first draft wrapped the command in backticks; when an operator pasted the banner verbatim into PowerShell, the backticks parsed as line-continuation and `(ECONNREFUSED)` as a sub-expression call. Plain-text form is copy-paste safe. Verified in live preview: API stopped → in-page `fetch('/api/v1/auth/register')` returned `503` + envelope, LoginPage banner DOM matched verbatim, console error stream flipped from `ApiError: Response not JSON (500)` to `ApiError: API server unreachable …` at the moment Vite picked up the config change; API restarted → same call returned `201` + `{ token, user }`. No edits to auth routes (`apps/api/src/routes/auth/index.ts` was sound), no new migrations, no dev seed-user script (explicitly declined — permanent fix only). ADR: [[decisions/2026-05-21-atlas-vite-proxy-api-offline-envelope]].

- [2026-05-29 — B4 follow-up: tooltip exit fade](log/2026-05-29-b4-tooltip-exit-fade.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes the last fade-related still-deferred bullet from the 2026-05-25 host-union-hover-tooltip ADR (deferred again on 2026-05-28): animated fade **out**. `PlanDataLayers.tsx` gets a third `useState` (`displayedUnion`) that mirrors `activeUnion = pinnedUnion ?? hoveredUnion` but lives one exit-animation longer, with `phase: 'entering' | 'exiting'` and a monotonic `key`. A `useEffect([activeUnion])` writes the mirror synchronously on non-null `activeUnion` (fresh `key` remounts the tooltip so the enter keyframe replays — covers re-enter during in-flight exit) and flips the mirror's phase to `'exiting'` on null `activeUnion`. A 180 ms safety `setTimeout` (120 ms anim + 60 ms slack) covers the `prefers-reduced-motion` short-circuit case where `animationend` never fires. Portal-render now reads `displayedUnion`, forwards `key`, `exiting`, and `onExited`, and forces `pinned={false}` during exit so the gold accent doesn't linger. `HostCanopyUnionTooltip.tsx` props extended with optional `exiting?` + `onExited?`; root `<div>` gets conditional `data-exiting='true'` and an `onAnimationEnd` handler that fires `onExited()` when `exiting === true` and `animationName.includes('tooltipFadeOut')` (CSS Modules scopes the keyframe name; `.includes` matches the scoped form). `HostCanopyUnionTooltip.module.css` adds `@keyframes tooltipFadeOut` (opacity 1→0, translateY 0→2px — the reverse of the enter keyframe); `.tooltip[data-exiting='true'] { animation: tooltipFadeOut 120ms ease-in forwards; }` — `forwards` holds the final state until React unmount. The `prefers-reduced-motion` media block extended to null both keyframes. New test asserts `data-exiting` forwarding + `onExited` fires on `tooltipFadeOut` animationend and NOT on unrelated keyframe names. Why not `useRef` or `useReducer`: refs don't trigger re-render (the portal-branch needs to subscribe); two-shape state machine doesn't justify reducer boilerplate. Why force `pinned=false` during exit: gold accent reads "sticky," fade reads "going away" — stacking confuses the surface. Invariants preserved: `pointer-events: none`, single-pin, single-tooltip, multi-feature fan-out, edge-clamp, enter fade, tap-outside dismiss. 69/69 vitest green (6 tooltip + 63 agroforestry). Touched files TS-clean. 2026-05-25 + 2026-05-28 ADR exit-fade bullets flipped to closed.

- [2026-05-20 — Phase C: Agent workforce + rotation→revenue bridge](log/2026-05-20-phase-c-agent-workforce-rotation-engine.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Two commits closing the Apricot-Lane Phase C boundary. **C.6 (`8418062a`)** widens `ClaudeClient.callAnthropic` to accept a `string | SystemBlock[]` and widens the return shape to `{ text, model, inputTokens, outputTokens }` (zero impact on the three existing public callers — string is wrapped in a single ephemeral-cached block as today). `SYSTEM_PROMPT` exported. New public `ClaudeClient.chatWithRole({ roleSystemAddendum, userMessage })` builds the canonical 2-block array — `[0]` cached Atlas base prompt with `cache_control: { type: 'ephemeral' }`, `[1]` the role addendum — and delegates to `callAnthropic`. New `apps/api/src/services/ai/agentRegistry.ts` exports `AgentRole` (`'agro-designer' | 'hydro-engineer' | 'general'`), a static role-prompt table, pure `routeIntent(text): AgentRole` (case-insensitive word-boundary keyword tally — hydro: `swale`, `keyline`, `pond`, `water`, `hydro`, `runoff`, `infiltration`, `drainage`, `riparian`, `aquifer`, `cistern`, `dam`, `creek`, `flood`; agro: `orchard`, `paddock`, `tree`, `plant`, `species`, `crop`, `pasture`, `grazing`, `livestock`, `rotation`, `cover crop`, `compost`, `silvopasture`; ties or zero → `'general'`), `resolveRole`, and `runAgent(input)` which composes the role addendum, calls `chatWithRole`, and parses any trailing `HANDOFF: <role> — <reason>` line (en-dash `—` or ASCII `--` separator) into `handoff: { to, reason } | null` (server does not auto-chain — caller decides). New route `POST /api/v1/ai/agent-chat` appended to `apps/api/src/routes/ai/index.ts` with `authenticate + resolveProjectRole` preHandlers (project-membership gate). 24-case test suite `apps/api/src/tests/aiAgents.test.ts` mirrors the `ClaudeClient.test.ts` global-`fetch`-stub pattern: `routeIntent` purity, `parseHandoff` positives + negatives + ASCII separator + malformed role, `resolveRole` precedence, `runAgent` end-to-end (composes the 2-block system array with the cached base prompt verbatim, autoRoutes, defaults to general, parses handoff, forwards usage tokens) and a direct `chatWithRole` unit test. **C.7 (`6a61d6cf`)** lands `apps/web/src/features/livestock/engine/rotationEngine.ts` (`computeRotationCalendar({ paddocks, herdSize, animalUnitMonths?, parasiteBreakDays = 60, grazeDaysPerPaddock = 3 }): RotationCalendar`) — wraps canonical `computeRotationCarryingCapacity` via a synthetic single-mob `RotationPlan` (every paddock in one cell group, `targetGrazeDays = grazeDaysPerPaddock`, `targetRestDays = parasiteBreakDays`) plus mob-grazed paddock list with per-paddock `stockingDensity = herdSize / areaHa` so the AU math is never forked; `cycleDays = grazeDaysPerPaddock × paddocks.length`; `recoveryDays = cycleDays − grazeDaysPerPaddock`; `annualAuDays = herdSize × 365`; `cyclesPerYear = floor(365 / cycleDays)`; `parasiteBreakCompliant = every entry's recoveryDays ≥ parasiteBreakDays`; degenerate input (no paddocks or `grazeDaysPerPaddock ≤ 0`) returns a well-formed zero calendar (`entries: []`, `cycleDays: 0`, `cyclesPerYear: 0`, vacuously compliant, `status: 'ok'`). New `apps/web/src/features/financial/engine/livestockRevenue.ts` (`buildLivestockRevenueStream(calendar, { pricePerAuDay, startYear = 1, maturityYear?, confidence = 'medium', assumptions?, id?, name? })`) — `annualRevenue.{low,mid,high} = pricePerAuDay.{...} × annualAuDays` (rounded); default 5-year build-up ramp `[0.2, 0.4, 0.65, 0.85, 1.0]` plateauing at 1.0 through year 10; `startYear` shifts the ramp; `assumptions[]` surfaces herd × 365 AU-days, rotation cycle + paddock count, parasite-break compliance line (✓ "Parasite-break floor met (Xd minimum rest)" vs ✗ "WARNING: parasite-break floor NOT met — recovery Yd < Xd"), utilization + status, plus caller-supplied lines; default `enterprise: 'livestock'`. The stream slots into `computeCashflow([], [stream], phases, horizon)` with **zero engine change**. `RotationScheduleCard.tsx` gains an additive "Cycle engine" summary block between the status pills row and the per-group timelines: `cyclesPerYear`, `annualAuDays` (locale-formatted), parasite-break compliance badge (green ≥ 60d / amber < 60d), and utilization % with status pill (`ok` / `tight` / `over`). Card doesn't track herd size today, so the block uses an implied-mob heuristic of ~1 AU/ha (`Math.max(1, round(totalHa))`) — clearly labelled in the header hint so stewards know it's a placeholder until herd-size capture lands. Existing ad-hoc moves table below is untouched per [[feedback_no_deletion]]; plan-driven `RotationSequenceCard.tsx` is left alone. 16 new tests (8 rotation-engine + 8 livestock-revenue) cover: 11 × 3-day graze → `cycleDays 33`, `recoveryDays 30`, parasite-break NOT met; 11 × 6-day graze → `cycleDays 66`, `recoveryDays 60`, compliant; 50 AU × 365 = 18,250 AU-days; 200-acre fixture at 1 AU / 2 acres → 36,500 AU-days; contiguous startDay sequence; degenerate empty + zero-herd paths; utilization roll-up; `annualRevenue.mid = pricePerAuDay.mid × annualAuDays`; enterprise tag; ramp 0 before startYear + monotone non-decreasing through plateau; startYear shift; WARNING / Parasite-break-floor-met assumptions; end-to-end `computeCashflow` integration (year-0 = 0, year-1 > 0, year-10 ≥ year-1). Gate: API tsc clean; `pnpm --filter @ogden/api run test` **653 passed / 3 skipped (656)** across 60 files; web tsc shows only pre-existing `StepBoundary.tsx(365,7)` `unknown→ReactNode` foreign-WIP error (verified via stash-baseline comparison); `pnpm --filter @ogden/web run test` **1620 passed (1620)** across 157 files (incl. 24 C.6 + 16 C.7 new cases). - [2026-05-27 — B4 follow-up: multi-feature fan-out on host-union tooltip](log/2026-05-27-b4-union-tooltip-multi-feature-fanout.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes the "Multi-feature fan-out when `resolveSilvopastureHosts` ever produces overlapping hosts" still-deferred bullet on the 2026-05-25 host-union-hover-tooltip ADR. The 2026-05-25 + 2026-05-26 ships both read only `e.features?.[0]` — when two silvopasture polygons spatially overlap (silvopastureHosts enumerator unions cropAreas + designElements with no dedup), the steward sees only one host's three m² values. `HostCanopyUnionTooltip` props refactored: new exported `HostBlockProps` interface; top-level shape becomes `{ point, entries: HostBlockProps[], pinned? }` (flat single-host fields removed, no backward-compat shim). Render loops `entries.map((e, i) => ...)` with `<hr className={styles.separator} role="separator" />` between consecutive blocks (single-host stacks omit the separator entirely — visually identical to the 2026-05-26 ship). `HostBlock` sub-component lifted local to the file. Edge-clamp `ESTIMATED_H` now `entries.length`-aware (`BASE_H + entries.length * PER_BLOCK_H` ~ 16 + 108·n) so the bottom-edge anchor flip keeps a 3-block tooltip on-screen at the gutter. CSS adds `.separator` hairline rule (`#f2ede3` family at 0.12 opacity against the dark glass). `PlanDataLayers` state widened: `hoveredUnion` / `pinnedUnion` carry `entries: HostBlock[]` (`HostBlock = HostBlockProps & { hostId: string }`); pinned additionally keeps a sorted `hostIds: string[]` for set-equality unpin. `unpackProps` → `unpackEntries` walks every entry in `e.features` (not `[0]`), filters by `properties.kind === 'host-canopy-union'`, dedups by `hostId` via `Set` (MapLibre can emit the same Feature twice when its source has multiple visible tiles intersecting the cursor). Click toggle now uses `sameHostIdSet` sorted-array equality: clicking a stack whose `hostIds` set matches the pinned stack's unpins; any other click replaces. Hover-suppression-while-pinned and ESC unpin unchanged. Portal render forwards `entries` instead of spread props. Why vertical stack, not tabs / chooser: any in-tooltip interactivity (tabs, hover-card-to-expand, chooser) would force `pointer-events: auto` and break the 2026-05-25 non-negotiable that the tooltip never steals `mouseleave` from the underlying union-fill. Stacking is the only design that holds the invariant. 1 new render test (two-host stack: both names visible, both sets of m² values rendered, exactly one `role="separator"` between); 4 existing tests migrated to length-1 `entries`. 5/5 tooltip + 63/63 agroforestry green; touched files TS-clean. 2026-05-25 ADR's multi-feature-fan-out bullet flipped open → closed.
- [2026-05-26 — B4 follow-up: click-to-pin tooltip + union-area centroid label](log/2026-05-26-b4-union-pin-and-label.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes two still-deferred bullets on the 2026-05-25 host-union-hover-tooltip ADR ("Click-to-pin variant" + "Union-area as a map label" — the label was originally carried forward from 2026-05-24). `PlanDataLayers` FC-builder now accumulates `hostCanopyUnionLabels` as a parallel point-Feature collection alongside `hostCanopyUnions`; each point anchored via `turf.pointOnFeature` (guaranteed-inside for concave / `MultiPolygon` shapes — `turf.centroid` can fall outside) carries `{ kind: 'host-canopy-union-label', hostId, unionAreaLabel }` where `unionAreaLabel` is the pre-formatted `` `${Math.round(union.unionAreaM2)} m²` `` string so the label, the tooltip, and `SilvopastureIntegrationCard` all share one formatter (no MapLibre `number-format` expression, no rounding drift). New `guild-host-canopy-union-label` source + `type: 'symbol'` layer at `minzoom: 17` with `text-field: ['get', 'unionAreaLabel']`, `text-size: 11`, `text-anchor: 'center'`, `text-allow-overlap: false`; paint mirrors the main label layer (`#f2ede3` text, `rgba(31, 29, 26, 0.85)` halo, halo-width 1.2); inserted **between** `guild-host-canopy-union-line` and `guild-member-canopy-fill` so member disks paint on top — the m² number is per-host context, not per-member identity. Click-to-pin via local `pinnedUnion` `useState` next to the existing `hoveredUnion` (single-pin model; same `{ point, props, hostId }` shape). Extended hover `useEffect`: `onMove` short-circuits when `pinnedUnion` is non-null (no jitter under cursor motion); new `onClick` on `guild-host-canopy-union-fill` toggles — same `hostId` unpins, different replaces; new `document keydown` clears on `Escape`. Cleanup `off`s + `removeEventListener` registered. Union-fill is **not** in `SELECTABLE_LAYERS` (confirmed), so click-to-pin does not also trigger selection clearing. Portal render picks `pinnedUnion ?? hoveredUnion` and forwards `pinned={!!pinnedUnion}` to the tooltip. `HostCanopyUnionTooltip` gains optional `pinned?: boolean` prop forwarded as `data-pinned="true"` on the root only when true; CSS adds `.tooltip[data-pinned='true'] { border-color: #c4a265; }` — brand-gold accent (same hue as the saved-overlap row) signals "this tooltip is sticky." `pointer-events: none` non-negotiable rule preserved — pinning does not change the contract that the tooltip never steals events. 1 new render test using `rerender` (existing 3 untouched); 4/4 tooltip + 63/63 agroforestry green; touched files TS-clean. 2026-05-25 ADR's "Click-to-pin variant" and "Union-area as map label" bullets flipped open → closed.

Header gains subtitle "Eight-dimension assessment, scored against your site layers." `isPendingData(item)` = `rating === 'Insufficient Data' && confidence === 'low'` swaps residual-only rows from "25 / Insufficient Data" to "— / Pending data" with muted dashed styling; FAO/USDA rows exempt (their `rating` is class-overridden). Verified on `/v3/project/mtc/observe` via DOM snapshot — 8 core rows, 6 diagnostic in details, 5 pending badges on cold-start state, zero console errors, HMR clean.
- [2026-05-20 — ContextBuilder hydration crash defensive guard (walkthrough gap #2)](log/2026-05-20-contextbuilder-hydration-crash-defensive-guard.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture` (no commit; staged). Closes gap #2 from [[log/2026-05-20-olos-new-user-journey-walkthrough]]. Two-line defensive guard in [`apps/web/src/features/ai/ContextBuilder.ts`](../apps/web/src/features/ai/ContextBuilder.ts): `p.species.map(...)` → `(p.species ?? []).map(...)` at line 84, `c.species.join(', ')` → `(c.species ?? []).join(', ')` at line 95. Root cause: `livestockStore` is `version: 1` with a no-op migrator, so v0 paddocks missing `species` hydrate unchanged and crash `aiEnrichment` on every boot. Verified by seeding a degraded paddock + crop via `preview_eval`, reloading Observe — all three `aiEnrichment` paths now reach the server API (failing only with the expected `AI features are not configured` env-var error). Livestock-store v2 migration flagged as deferred follow-up.

- [2026-05-21 — Habitat-feature unification into Plan design elements (Slices 1-3 landed then dropped by external rebase, Slice 4 partial)](log/2026-05-21-habitat-feature-unification-into-design-elements.md) — Steward-chosen direction for the A2 habitat commitments (owl/nest boxes, raptor perches, hedgerows, insectary strips, brush piles, snags, wildlife ponds): unify into Plan `DesignElement` subtypes under a new `habitat` category in `elementCatalog.ts`. Three slices landed and verified — **Slice 1** (`43dd56a9`) new category + 7 first-class kinds (`owl-box` / `raptor-perch` / `nest-box` / `brush-pile` / `snag` / `insectary-strip` / `wetland-edge`) + 6 colour tokens + Lucide icons + explicit tool-dispatch switch cases (discovered against plan assumption: dispatch is NOT fully catalog-driven), template-literal arm on `MapToolId`, `TOOL_GROUPS` `'habitat-allocation'` rail; **Slice 2** (`933c0709`) optional `habitatMetadata?` slot on `DesignElement` (scoped down from per-kind popover — schema-only suffices for all four downstream consumers); **Slice 3** (`ac11dfa6`) extends `BeneficialStructureKind` + `BENEFICIAL_STRUCTURE_FUNCTIONS` with cited categories for each new kind (Cornell NestWatch / Audubon Working Lands / USDA NRCS / USDA Forest Service PNW-GTR-181 / Xerces CSP 422 — preserves B5 cite-every-claim covenant) and adds 7 new aggregate fields + 7 new structural-loop arms to `beneficialHabitatMath`, updating `structuralPoints` to `hedgerowM/100 + pondM²/500 + shrubs + owlBoxes + raptorPerches + nestBoxes + brushPiles + snags + insectaryStripM/100 + wetlandEdgeM²/500`; envelope clamp unchanged so effect on existing projects is monotonic increase. 37 vitest specs added across catalog + math suites, all green at commit time. **Slice 4** (uncommitted) introduced pure-selector module `apps/web/src/features/biodiversity/habitatCommitments.ts` (10-kind `HabitatCommitmentTally` shape via turf line-length / polygon-area helpers) with 10-spec colocated test, an additive "Planned habitat commitments" sub-panel on `BiodiversityMonitorCard`, and a read-only "Placed on map" summary block at the top of `FeatureInventoryPanel` (legacy scalar add-form retained as soft-deprecated path; destructive v1→v2 bridge migration deliberately skipped to keep the slice rebase-safe). **Slice 5** (D0 spine seeder via `habitatFeatureSpineSync.ts`) not started. After commits landed, an external interactive rebase replayed `feat/atlas-permaculture` onto a new base and dropped all three slice commits from the resulting history (the exact failure mode [[feedback-commit-immediately-on-rebased-branches]] warns about — committed work survives rebases unless a pick is explicitly dropped, which here it was); Slice 4 file edits + the two new untracked files were also wiped by the subsequent hard-reset. Local now matches `origin/feat/atlas-permaculture` exactly. Re-application path: plan checked into `~/.claude/plans/habitat-features-need-a-lively-oasis.md`, file inventory in the linked log entry, all per-file content documented.
- [2026-05-24 — Stage compass wheel fills its space + True North banner clears the header](log/2026-05-24-compass-wheel-fit-and-true-north-banner.md) — Two Observe-compass UI-polish fixes (shared across Observe/Plan/Act). Banner: was `position:fixed; top:var(--space-4)` behind the 48px AppShell header (higher z-index) so its top half clipped → pinned to `calc(48px + var(--space-3))`. Wheel: was double-capped (`.wheelHost max-width:440px` + shared `.mcw-svg max-width:540px`) → height-driven square fit (`height:100%; aspect-ratio:1; max-width:100%`) + `:global(.mcw-svg)` cap override, sizing to `min(width,height)`. Verified live at 1920/1137/375 (944/449/300px, square, no overflow). One explicit-path commit `73d2678e`, CSS-only, covenant clean.
- [2026-05-24 — Global wheel fill-to-fit standard + proportional center overlays](log/2026-05-24-global-wheel-fit-standard-and-proportional-overlays.md) — Made the same-day wheel fit ([[log/2026-05-24-compass-wheel-fit-and-true-north-banner]]) the **global standard** via a shared CSS module `apps/web/src/components/wheel-shared/wheelFit.module.css`, consumed through CSS-Modules `composes` (zero TSX changes). Two layout families forced a split: **dedicated full-bleed** surfaces (Observe/Plan/Act + True North) get `.fillHost` true height-driven fit + `.quiet` biophilic fills; **content-flow** surfaces (Cycle page, OPA dashboard) get `.relaxedHost` (fixed px cap removed, width-driven so stacked siblings stay intact). Center overlay made proportional: `.hotspot` 29.5% of wheel (tracks the ~28% hub), `.hint` `top:103.8%` resolved against the hotspot **button** (not the host) — the subtle bug, originally mis-set to 65.9%. Six files (1 new + 5 edits), CSS-only, covenant clean. Verified live: Observe 944/300px + True North 777px, hotspot centered, hint clears hub at both sizes; `tsc` + `vite build` exit 0.
